    def get_result(self) -> ResultType:
        """Get the result(s) for this hook call.

        If the hook was marked as a ``firstresult`` only a single value
        will be returned, otherwise a list of results.
        """
        __tracebackhide__ = True
        exc = self._exception
        tb = self._traceback
        if exc is None:
            return cast(ResultType, self._result)
        else:

    def __call__(self, **kwargs: object) -> Any:
        """Call the hook.

        Only accepts keyword arguments, which should match the hook
        specification.

        Returns the result(s) of calling all registered plugins, see
        :ref:`calling`.
        """
        assert not self.is_historic(), (
            "Cannot directly call a historic hook - use call_historic instead."
        )
        self._verify_all_args_are_provided(kwargs)
        firstresult = self.spec.opts.get("firstresult", False) if self.spec else False
        # Copy because plugins may register other plugins during iteration (#438).

    def _multicall(
        hook_name: str,
        hook_impls: Sequence[HookImpl],
        caller_kwargs: Mapping[str, object],
        firstresult: bool,
    ) -> object | list[object]:
        """Execute a call into multiple python functions/methods and return the
        result(s).

        ``caller_kwargs`` comes from HookCaller.__call__().
        """
        __tracebackhide__ = True
        results: list[object] = []
        exception = None
        try:  # run impl and wrapper setup functions in a loop
            teardowns: list[Teardown] = []
            try:
                for hook_impl in reversed(hook_impls):
                    try:
                        args = [caller_kwargs[argname] for argname in hook_impl.argnames]
                    except KeyError as e:
                        # coverage bug - this is tested
                        for argname in hook_impl.argnames:  # pragma: no cover
                            if argname not in caller_kwargs:
                                raise HookCallError(
                                    f"hook call must provide argument {argname!r}"
                                ) from e

                    if hook_impl.hookwrapper:
                        function_gen = run_old_style_hookwrapper(hook_impl, hook_name, args)

                        next(function_gen)  # first yield
                        teardowns.append(function_gen)

                    elif hook_impl.wrapper:
                        try:
                            # If this cast is not valid, a type error is raised below,
                            # which is the desired response.
                            res = hook_impl.function(*args)
                            function_gen = cast(Generator[None, object, object], res)
                            next(function_gen)  # first yield
                            teardowns.append(function_gen)
                        except StopIteration:
                            _raise_wrapfail(function_gen, "did not yield")
                    else:
                        res = hook_impl.function(*args)
                        if res is not None:
                            results.append(res)
                            if firstresult:  # halt further impl calls
                                break
            except BaseException as exc:
                exception = exc
        finally:
            if firstresult:  # first result hooks return a single value
                result = results[0] if results else None
            else:
                result = results

            # run all wrapper post-yield blocks
            for teardown in reversed(teardowns):
                try:
                    if exception is not None:
                        try:
                            teardown.throw(exception)
                        except RuntimeError as re:
                            # StopIteration from generator causes RuntimeError
                            # even for coroutine usage - see #544
                            if (
                                isinstance(exception, StopIteration)
                                and re.__cause__ is exception
                            ):
                                teardown.close()
                                continue
                            else:
                                raise
                    else:
                        teardown.send(result)
                    # Following is unreachable for a well behaved hook wrapper.
                    # Try to force finalizers otherwise postponed till GC action.
                    # Note: close() may raise if generator handles GeneratorExit.
                    teardown.close()
                except StopIteration as si:
                    result = si.value
                    exception = None
                    continue
                except BaseException as e:
                    exception = e
                    continue
                _raise_wrapfail(teardown, "has second yield")

        if exception is not None:
>           raise exception

    def __call__(self, **kwargs: object) -> Any:
        """Call the hook.

        Only accepts keyword arguments, which should match the hook
        specification.

        Returns the result(s) of calling all registered plugins, see
        :ref:`calling`.
        """
        assert not self.is_historic(), (
            "Cannot directly call a historic hook - use call_historic instead."
        )
        self._verify_all_args_are_provided(kwargs)
        firstresult = self.spec.opts.get("firstresult", False) if self.spec else False
        # Copy because plugins may register other plugins during iteration (#438).

hook_name = 'pytest_runtest_call'
hook_impls = [<HookImpl plugin_name='threadexception', plugin=<module '_pytest.threadexception' from '/app/.nox/tests-3-11/lib/pyth...ture_fixture=None>>, <HookImpl plugin_name='_cov', plugin=<pytest_cov.plugin.CovPlugin object at 0x7f6f7b5a4a10>>, ...]
caller_kwargs = {'item': <Function test_uv_install[python3.12-True]>}
firstresult = False

    def _multicall(
        hook_name: str,
        hook_impls: Sequence[HookImpl],
        caller_kwargs: Mapping[str, object],
        firstresult: bool,
    ) -> object | list[object]:
        """Execute a call into multiple python functions/methods and return the
        result(s).

        ``caller_kwargs`` comes from HookCaller.__call__().
        """
        __tracebackhide__ = True
        results: list[object] = []
        exception = None
        try:  # run impl and wrapper setup functions in a loop
            teardowns: list[Teardown] = []
            try:
                for hook_impl in reversed(hook_impls):
                    try:
                        args = [caller_kwargs[argname] for argname in hook_impl.argnames]
                    except KeyError as e:
                        # coverage bug - this is tested
                        for argname in hook_impl.argnames:  # pragma: no cover
                            if argname not in caller_kwargs:
                                raise HookCallError(
                                    f"hook call must provide argument {argname!r}"
                                ) from e

                    if hook_impl.hookwrapper:
                        function_gen = run_old_style_hookwrapper(hook_impl, hook_name, args)

                        next(function_gen)  # first yield
                        teardowns.append(function_gen)

                    elif hook_impl.wrapper:
                        try:
                            # If this cast is not valid, a type error is raised below,
                            # which is the desired response.
                            res = hook_impl.function(*args)
                            function_gen = cast(Generator[None, object, object], res)
                            next(function_gen)  # first yield
                            teardowns.append(function_gen)
                        except StopIteration:
                            _raise_wrapfail(function_gen, "did not yield")
                    else:
                        res = hook_impl.function(*args)
                        if res is not None:
                            results.append(res)
                            if firstresult:  # halt further impl calls
                                break
            except BaseException as exc:
                exception = exc
        finally:
            if firstresult:  # first result hooks return a single value
                result = results[0] if results else None
            else:
                result = results

            # run all wrapper post-yield blocks
            for teardown in reversed(teardowns):
                try:
                    if exception is not None:
                        try:
                            teardown.throw(exception)
                        except RuntimeError as re:
                            # StopIteration from generator causes RuntimeError
                            # even for coroutine usage - see #544
                            if (
                                isinstance(exception, StopIteration)
                                and re.__cause__ is exception
                            ):
                                teardown.close()
                                continue
                            else:
                                raise
                    else:
                        teardown.send(result)
                    # Following is unreachable for a well behaved hook wrapper.
                    # Try to force finalizers otherwise postponed till GC action.
                    # Note: close() may raise if generator handles GeneratorExit.
                    teardown.close()
                except StopIteration as si:
                    result = si.value
                    exception = None
                    continue
                except BaseException as e:
                    exception = e
                    continue
                _raise_wrapfail(teardown, "has second yield")

        if exception is not None:
>           raise exception

args = [<Function test_uv_install[python3.12-True]>]

    def run_old_style_hookwrapper(
        hook_impl: HookImpl, hook_name: str, args: Sequence[object]
    ) -> Teardown:
        """
        backward compatibility wrapper to run a old style hookwrapper as a wrapper
        """

        teardown: Teardown = cast(Teardown, hook_impl.function(*args))
        try:
            next(teardown)
        except StopIteration:
            _raise_wrapfail(teardown, "did not yield")
        try:
            res = yield
            result = Result(res, None)
        except BaseException as exc:
            result = Result(None, exc)
        try:
            teardown.send(result)
        except StopIteration:
            pass
        except BaseException as e:
            _warn_teardown_exception(hook_name, hook_impl, e)
            raise
        else:
            _raise_wrapfail(teardown, "has second yield")
        finally:
            teardown.close()
>       return result.get_result()
               ^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^

self = <pluggy._result.Result object at 0x7f6f79d68c80>

    def get_result(self) -> ResultType:
        """Get the result(s) for this hook call.

        If the hook was marked as a ``firstresult`` only a single value
        will be returned, otherwise a list of results.
        """
        __tracebackhide__ = True
        exc = self._exception
        tb = self._traceback
        if exc is None:
            return cast(ResultType, self._result)
        else:
>           raise exc.with_traceback(tb)

hook_name = 'pytest_pyfunc_call'
hook_impls = [<HookImpl plugin_name='python', plugin=<module '_pytest.python' from '/app/.nox/tests-3-11/lib/python3.11/site-packag...plugin=<module 'anyio.pytest_plugin' from '/app/.nox/tests-3-11/lib/python3.11/site-packages/anyio/pytest_plugin.py'>>]
caller_kwargs = {'pyfuncitem': <Function test_uv_install[python3.12-True]>}
firstresult = True

    def _multicall(
        hook_name: str,
        hook_impls: Sequence[HookImpl],
        caller_kwargs: Mapping[str, object],
        firstresult: bool,
    ) -> object | list[object]:
        """Execute a call into multiple python functions/methods and return the
        result(s).

        ``caller_kwargs`` comes from HookCaller.__call__().
        """
        __tracebackhide__ = True
        results: list[object] = []
        exception = None
        try:  # run impl and wrapper setup functions in a loop
            teardowns: list[Teardown] = []
            try:
                for hook_impl in reversed(hook_impls):
                    try:
                        args = [caller_kwargs[argname] for argname in hook_impl.argnames]
                    except KeyError as e:
                        # coverage bug - this is tested
                        for argname in hook_impl.argnames:  # pragma: no cover
                            if argname not in caller_kwargs:
                                raise HookCallError(
                                    f"hook call must provide argument {argname!r}"
                                ) from e

                    if hook_impl.hookwrapper:
                        function_gen = run_old_style_hookwrapper(hook_impl, hook_name, args)

                        next(function_gen)  # first yield
                        teardowns.append(function_gen)

                    elif hook_impl.wrapper:
                        try:
                            # If this cast is not valid, a type error is raised below,
                            # which is the desired response.
                            res = hook_impl.function(*args)
                            function_gen = cast(Generator[None, object, object], res)
                            next(function_gen)  # first yield
                            teardowns.append(function_gen)
                        except StopIteration:
                            _raise_wrapfail(function_gen, "did not yield")
                    else:
                        res = hook_impl.function(*args)
                        if res is not None:
                            results.append(res)
                            if firstresult:  # halt further impl calls
                                break
            except BaseException as exc:
                exception = exc
        finally:
            if firstresult:  # first result hooks return a single value
                result = results[0] if results else None
            else:
                result = results

            # run all wrapper post-yield blocks
            for teardown in reversed(teardowns):
                try:
                    if exception is not None:
                        try:
                            teardown.throw(exception)
                        except RuntimeError as re:
                            # StopIteration from generator causes RuntimeError
                            # even for coroutine usage - see #544
                            if (
                                isinstance(exception, StopIteration)
                                and re.__cause__ is exception
                            ):
                                teardown.close()
                                continue
                            else:
                                raise
                    else:
                        teardown.send(result)
                    # Following is unreachable for a well behaved hook wrapper.
                    # Try to force finalizers otherwise postponed till GC action.
                    # Note: close() may raise if generator handles GeneratorExit.
                    teardown.close()
                except StopIteration as si:
                    result = si.value
                    exception = None
                    continue
                except BaseException as e:
                    exception = e
                    continue
                _raise_wrapfail(teardown, "has second yield")

        if exception is not None:
>           raise exception

hook_name = 'pytest_runtest_call'

firstresult = False

    def _multicall(
        hook_name: str,
        hook_impls: Sequence[HookImpl],
        caller_kwargs: Mapping[str, object],
        firstresult: bool,
    ) -> object | list[object]:
        """Execute a call into multiple python functions/methods and return the
        result(s).

        ``caller_kwargs`` comes from HookCaller.__call__().
        """
        __tracebackhide__ = True
        results: list[object] = []
        exception = None
        try:  # run impl and wrapper setup functions in a loop
            teardowns: list[Teardown] = []
            try:
                for hook_impl in reversed(hook_impls):
                    try:
                        args = [caller_kwargs[argname] for argname in hook_impl.argnames]
                    except KeyError as e:
                        # coverage bug - this is tested
                        for argname in hook_impl.argnames:  # pragma: no cover
                            if argname not in caller_kwargs:
                                raise HookCallError(
                                    f"hook call must provide argument {argname!r}"
                                ) from e

                    if hook_impl.hookwrapper:
                        function_gen = run_old_style_hookwrapper(hook_impl, hook_name, args)

                        next(function_gen)  # first yield
                        teardowns.append(function_gen)

                    elif hook_impl.wrapper:
                        try:
                            # If this cast is not valid, a type error is raised below,
                            # which is the desired response.
                            res = hook_impl.function(*args)
                            function_gen = cast(Generator[None, object, object], res)
                            next(function_gen)  # first yield
                            teardowns.append(function_gen)
                        except StopIteration:
                            _raise_wrapfail(function_gen, "did not yield")
                    else:
                        res = hook_impl.function(*args)
                        if res is not None:
                            results.append(res)
                            if firstresult:  # halt further impl calls
                                break
            except BaseException as exc:
                exception = exc
        finally:
            if firstresult:  # first result hooks return a single value
                result = results[0] if results else None
            else:
                result = results

            # run all wrapper post-yield blocks
            for teardown in reversed(teardowns):
                try:
                    if exception is not None:
                        try:
>                           teardown.throw(exception)

/app/.nox/tests-3-11/lib/python3.11/site-packages/pluggy/_callers.py:139:

hook_impl = <HookImpl plugin_name='_cov', plugin=<pytest_cov.plugin.CovPlugin object at 0x7f6f7b5a4a10>>
hook_name = 'pytest_runtest_call'
args = [<Function test_create_reuse_venv_environment>]

    def run_old_style_hookwrapper(
        hook_impl: HookImpl, hook_name: str, args: Sequence[object]
    ) -> Teardown:
        """
        backward compatibility wrapper to run a old style hookwrapper as a wrapper
        """

        teardown: Teardown = cast(Teardown, hook_impl.function(*args))
        try:
            next(teardown)
        except StopIteration:
            _raise_wrapfail(teardown, "did not yield")
        try:
            res = yield
            result = Result(res, None)
        except BaseException as exc:
            result = Result(None, exc)
        try:
            teardown.send(result)
        except StopIteration:
            pass
        except BaseException as e:
            _warn_teardown_exception(hook_name, hook_impl, e)
            raise
        else:
            _raise_wrapfail(teardown, "has second yield")
        finally:
            teardown.close()
>       return result.get_result()
               ^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^

    def get_result(self) -> ResultType:
        """Get the result(s) for this hook call.

        If the hook was marked as a ``firstresult`` only a single value
        will be returned, otherwise a list of results.
        """
        __tracebackhide__ = True
        exc = self._exception
        tb = self._traceback
        if exc is None:
            return cast(ResultType, self._result)
        else:

    def __call__(self, **kwargs: object) -> Any:
        """Call the hook.

        Only accepts keyword arguments, which should match the hook
        specification.

        Returns the result(s) of calling all registered plugins, see
        :ref:`calling`.
        """
        assert not self.is_historic(), (
            "Cannot directly call a historic hook - use call_historic instead."
        )
        self._verify_all_args_are_provided(kwargs)
        firstresult = self.spec.opts.get("firstresult", False) if self.spec else False

                    try:
                        args = [caller_kwargs[argname] for argname in hook_impl.argnames]
                    except KeyError as e:
                        # coverage bug - this is tested
                        for argname in hook_impl.argnames:  # pragma: no cover
                            if argname not in caller_kwargs:
                                raise HookCallError(
                                    f"hook call must provide argument {argname!r}"
                                ) from e

                    if hook_impl.hookwrapper:
                        function_gen = run_old_style_hookwrapper(hook_impl, hook_name, args)

                        next(function_gen)  # first yield
                        teardowns.append(function_gen)

                    elif hook_impl.wrapper:
                        try:
                            # If this cast is not valid, a type error is raised below,
                            # which is the desired response.
                            res = hook_impl.function(*args)
                            function_gen = cast(Generator[None, object, object], res)
                            next(function_gen)  # first yield
                            teardowns.append(function_gen)
                        except StopIteration:
                            _raise_wrapfail(function_gen, "did not yield")
                    else:
                        res = hook_impl.function(*args)
                        if res is not None:
                            results.append(res)
                            if firstresult:  # halt further impl calls
                                break
            except BaseException as exc:
                exception = exc
        finally:
            if firstresult:  # first result hooks return a single value
                result = results[0] if results else None
            else:
                result = results

            # run all wrapper post-yield blocks
            for teardown in reversed(teardowns):
                try:
                    if exception is not None:
                        try:
                            teardown.throw(exception)
                        except RuntimeError as re:
                            # StopIteration from generator causes RuntimeError
                            # even for coroutine usage - see #544
                            if (
                                isinstance(exception, StopIteration)
                                and re.__cause__ is exception
                            ):
                                teardown.close()
                                continue
                            else:
                                raise
                    else:
                        teardown.send(result)
                    # Following is unreachable for a well behaved hook wrapper.
                    # Try to force finalizers otherwise postponed till GC action.
                    # Note: close() may raise if generator handles GeneratorExit.
                    teardown.close()
                except StopIteration as si:
                    result = si.value
                    exception = None
                    continue
                except BaseException as e:
                    exception = e
                    continue
                _raise_wrapfail(teardown, "has second yield")

        if exception is not None:
>           raise exception

/app/tests/test_virtualenv.py:999:

self = <nox.virtualenv.VirtualEnv object at 0x7f6f79be1550>

    def create(self) -> bool:
        """Create the virtualenv or venv."""
        if not self._clean_location():
            logger.debug(
                f"Reusing existing virtual environment at {self.location_name}."
            )

            self._reused = True

            return False

        if self.venv_backend == "virtualenv":
            cmd = [
                sys.executable,
                "-m",
                "virtualenv",
                self.location,
                "--no-periodic-update",
            ]
            if self.interpreter:
                cmd.extend(["-p", self._resolved_interpreter])
        elif self.venv_backend == "uv":
            cmd = [
                UV,
                "venv",
                "-p",
                self._resolved_interpreter if self.interpreter else sys.executable,
                self.location,
            ]
            if version.Version("0.8") <= UV_VERSION:
                cmd += ["--clear"]
        else:
            cmd = [self._resolved_interpreter, "-m", "venv", self.location]
        cmd.extend(self.venv_params)

        resolved_interpreter_name = os.path.basename(self._resolved_interpreter)

        logger.info(
            f"Creating virtual environment ({self.venv_backend}) using"
            f" {resolved_interpreter_name} in {self.location_name}"
        )
>       nox.command.run(cmd, silent=True, log=nox.options.verbose or False)

args = ['-m', 'venv', '/app/.nox/tests-3-11/tmp/pytest-of-root/pytest-0/test_create_reuse_venv_environ0/venv']

    def run(
        args: Sequence[str | os.PathLike[str]],
        *,
        env: Mapping[str, str | None] | None = None,
        silent: bool = False,
        paths: Sequence[str | os.PathLike[str]] | None = None,
        success_codes: Iterable[int] | None = None,
        log: bool = True,
        external: ExternalType = False,
        stdout: int | IO[str] | None = None,
        stderr: int | IO[str] | None = subprocess.STDOUT,
        interrupt_timeout: float | None = DEFAULT_INTERRUPT_TIMEOUT,
        terminate_timeout: float | None = DEFAULT_TERMINATE_TIMEOUT,
    ) -> str | bool:
        """Run a command-line program."""

        if success_codes is None:
            success_codes = [0]

        cmd, args = args[0], args[1:]
        full_cmd = f"{cmd} {_shlex_join(args)}"

        cmd_path = which(os.fspath(cmd), paths)
        str_args = [os.fspath(arg) for arg in args]

        if log:
            logger.info(full_cmd)

            is_external_tool = paths is not None and not any(
                cmd_path.startswith(str(path)) for path in paths
            )
            if is_external_tool:
                if external == "error":
                    logger.error(
                        f"Error: {cmd} is not installed into the virtualenv, it is located"
                        f" at {cmd_path}. Pass external=True into run() to explicitly allow"
                        " this."
                    )
                    msg = "External program disallowed."
                    raise CommandFailed(msg)
                if external is False:
                    logger.warning(
                        f"Warning: {cmd} is not installed into the virtualenv, it is"
                        f" located at {cmd_path}. This might cause issues! Pass"
                        " external=True into run() to silence this message."
                    )

        env = _clean_env(env)

        try:
            return_code, output = popen(
                [cmd_path, *str_args],
                silent=silent,
                env=env,
                stdout=stdout,
                stderr=stderr,
                interrupt_timeout=interrupt_timeout,
                terminate_timeout=terminate_timeout,
            )

            if return_code not in success_codes:
                suffix = ":" if (silent and output) else ""
                logger.error(
                    f"Command {full_cmd} failed with exit code {return_code}{suffix}"
                )

                if silent and output:
                    logger.error(output)

                msg = f"Returned code {return_code}"
>               raise CommandFailed(msg)

hook_name = 'pytest_runtest_call'
hook_impls = [<HookImpl plugin_name='threadexception', plugin=<module '_pytest.threadexception' from '/app/.nox/tests-3-11/lib/pyth...ture_fixture=None>>, <HookImpl plugin_name='_cov', plugin=<pytest_cov.plugin.CovPlugin object at 0x7f6f7b5a4a10>>, ...]
caller_kwargs = {'item': <Function test_create_venv_backend>}
firstresult = False

    def _multicall(
        hook_name: str,
        hook_impls: Sequence[HookImpl],
        caller_kwargs: Mapping[str, object],
        firstresult: bool,
    ) -> object | list[object]:
        """Execute a call into multiple python functions/methods and return the
        result(s).

        ``caller_kwargs`` comes from HookCaller.__call__().
        """
        __tracebackhide__ = True
        results: list[object] = []
        exception = None
        try:  # run impl and wrapper setup functions in a loop
            teardowns: list[Teardown] = []
            try:
                for hook_impl in reversed(hook_impls):
                    try:
                        args = [caller_kwargs[argname] for argname in hook_impl.argnames]
                    except KeyError as e:
                        # coverage bug - this is tested
                        for argname in hook_impl.argnames:  # pragma: no cover
                            if argname not in caller_kwargs:
                                raise HookCallError(
                                    f"hook call must provide argument {argname!r}"
                                ) from e

                    if hook_impl.hookwrapper:
                        function_gen = run_old_style_hookwrapper(hook_impl, hook_name, args)

                        next(function_gen)  # first yield
                        teardowns.append(function_gen)

                    elif hook_impl.wrapper:
                        try:
                            # If this cast is not valid, a type error is raised below,
                            # which is the desired response.
                            res = hook_impl.function(*args)
                            function_gen = cast(Generator[None, object, object], res)
                            next(function_gen)  # first yield
                            teardowns.append(function_gen)
                        except StopIteration:
                            _raise_wrapfail(function_gen, "did not yield")
                    else:
                        res = hook_impl.function(*args)
                        if res is not None:
                            results.append(res)
                            if firstresult:  # halt further impl calls
                                break
            except BaseException as exc:
                exception = exc
        finally:
            if firstresult:  # first result hooks return a single value
                result = results[0] if results else None
            else:
                result = results

            # run all wrapper post-yield blocks
            for teardown in reversed(teardowns):
                try:
                    if exception is not None:
                        try:
                            teardown.throw(exception)
                        except RuntimeError as re:
                            # StopIteration from generator causes RuntimeError
                            # even for coroutine usage - see #544
                            if (
                                isinstance(exception, StopIteration)
                                and re.__cause__ is exception
                            ):
                                teardown.close()
                                continue
                            else:
                                raise
                    else:
                        teardown.send(result)
                    # Following is unreachable for a well behaved hook wrapper.
                    # Try to force finalizers otherwise postponed till GC action.
                    # Note: close() may raise if generator handles GeneratorExit.
                    teardown.close()
                except StopIteration as si:
                    result = si.value
                    exception = None
                    continue
                except BaseException as e:
                    exception = e
                    continue
                _raise_wrapfail(teardown, "has second yield")

        if exception is not None:
>           raise exception

    def run_old_style_hookwrapper(
        hook_impl: HookImpl, hook_name: str, args: Sequence[object]
    ) -> Teardown:
        """
        backward compatibility wrapper to run a old style hookwrapper as a wrapper
        """

        teardown: Teardown = cast(Teardown, hook_impl.function(*args))
        try:
            next(teardown)
        except StopIteration:
            _raise_wrapfail(teardown, "did not yield")
        try:
            res = yield
            result = Result(res, None)
        except BaseException as exc:
            result = Result(None, exc)
        try:
            teardown.send(result)
        except StopIteration:
            pass
        except BaseException as e:
            _warn_teardown_exception(hook_name, hook_impl, e)
            raise
        else:
            _raise_wrapfail(teardown, "has second yield")
        finally:
            teardown.close()
>       return result.get_result()

    def get_result(self) -> ResultType:
        """Get the result(s) for this hook call.

        If the hook was marked as a ``firstresult`` only a single value
        will be returned, otherwise a list of results.

        else:

    def __call__(self, **kwargs: object) -> Any:
        """Call the hook.

        Only accepts keyword arguments, which should match the hook
        specification.

        Returns the result(s) of calling all registered plugins, see
        :ref:`calling`.

            "Cannot directly call a historic hook - use call_historic instead."
        )

    def _multicall(
        hook_name: str,
        hook_impls: Sequence[HookImpl],
        caller_kwargs: Mapping[str, object],
        firstresult: bool,
    ) -> object | list[object]:
        """Execute a call into multiple python functions/methods and return the
        result(s).

        ``caller_kwargs`` comes from HookCaller.__call__().
        """
        __tracebackhide__ = True
        results: list[object] = []
        exception = None
        try:  # run impl and wrapper setup functions in a loop
            teardowns: list[Teardown] = []
            try:
                for hook_impl in reversed(hook_impls):
                    try:
                        args = [caller_kwargs[argname] for argname in hook_impl.argnames]
                    except KeyError as e:
                        # coverage bug - this is tested
                        for argname in hook_impl.argnames:  # pragma: no cover
                            if argname not in caller_kwargs:
                                raise HookCallError(
                                    f"hook call must provide argument {argname!r}"
                                ) from e

                    if hook_impl.hookwrapper:
                        function_gen = run_old_style_hookwrapper(hook_impl, hook_name, args)

                        next(function_gen)  # first yield
                        teardowns.append(function_gen)

                    elif hook_impl.wrapper:
                        try:
                            # If this cast is not valid, a type error is raised below,
                            # which is the desired response.
                            res = hook_impl.function(*args)
                            function_gen = cast(Generator[None, object, object], res)
                            next(function_gen)  # first yield
                            teardowns.append(function_gen)
                        except StopIteration:
                            _raise_wrapfail(function_gen, "did not yield")
                    else:
                        res = hook_impl.function(*args)
                        if res is not None:
                            results.append(res)
                            if firstresult:  # halt further impl calls
                                break
            except BaseException as exc:
                exception = exc
        finally:
            if firstresult:  # first result hooks return a single value
                result = results[0] if results else None
            else:
                result = results

            # run all wrapper post-yield blocks
            for teardown in reversed(teardowns):
                try:
                    if exception is not None:
                        try:
                            teardown.throw(exception)
                        except RuntimeError as re:
                            # StopIteration from generator causes RuntimeError
                            # even for coroutine usage - see #544
                            if (
                                isinstance(exception, StopIteration)
                                and re.__cause__ is exception
                            ):
                                teardown.close()
                                continue
                            else:
                                raise
                    else:
                        teardown.send(result)
                    # Following is unreachable for a well behaved hook wrapper.
                    # Try to force finalizers otherwise postponed till GC action.
                    # Note: close() may raise if generator handles GeneratorExit.
                    teardown.close()
                except StopIteration as si:
                    result = si.value
                    exception = None
                    continue
                except BaseException as e:
                    exception = e
                    continue
                _raise_wrapfail(teardown, "has second yield")

        if exception is not None:
>           raise exception

/app/tests/test_virtualenv.py:1092:

self = <nox.virtualenv.VirtualEnv object at 0x7f6f79b86810>

    def create(self) -> bool:
        """Create the virtualenv or venv."""
        if not self._clean_location():
            logger.debug(
                f"Reusing existing virtual environment at {self.location_name}."
            )

            self._reused = True

            return False

        if self.venv_backend == "virtualenv":
            cmd = [
                sys.executable,
                "-m",
                "virtualenv",
                self.location,
                "--no-periodic-update",
            ]
            if self.interpreter:
                cmd.extend(["-p", self._resolved_interpreter])
        elif self.venv_backend == "uv":
            cmd = [
                UV,
                "venv",
                "-p",
                self._resolved_interpreter if self.interpreter else sys.executable,
                self.location,
            ]
            if version.Version("0.8") <= UV_VERSION:
                cmd += ["--clear"]
        else:
            cmd = [self._resolved_interpreter, "-m", "venv", self.location]
        cmd.extend(self.venv_params)

        resolved_interpreter_name = os.path.basename(self._resolved_interpreter)

        logger.info(
            f"Creating virtual environment ({self.venv_backend}) using"
            f" {resolved_interpreter_name} in {self.location_name}"
        )
>       nox.command.run(cmd, silent=True, log=nox.options.verbose or False)

/app/nox/virtualenv.py:817:
_ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _

args = ['-m', 'venv', '/app/.nox/tests-3-11/tmp/pytest-of-root/pytest-0/test_create_venv_backend0/venv']

    def run(
        args: Sequence[str | os.PathLike[str]],
        *,
        env: Mapping[str, str | None] | None = None,
        silent: bool = False,
        paths: Sequence[str | os.PathLike[str]] | None = None,
        success_codes: Iterable[int] | None = None,
        log: bool = True,
        external: ExternalType = False,
        stdout: int | IO[str] | None = None,
        stderr: int | IO[str] | None = subprocess.STDOUT,
        interrupt_timeout: float | None = DEFAULT_INTERRUPT_TIMEOUT,
        terminate_timeout: float | None = DEFAULT_TERMINATE_TIMEOUT,
    ) -> str | bool:
        """Run a command-line program."""

        if success_codes is None:
            success_codes = [0]

        cmd, args = args[0], args[1:]
        full_cmd = f"{cmd} {_shlex_join(args)}"

        cmd_path = which(os.fspath(cmd), paths)
        str_args = [os.fspath(arg) for arg in args]

        if log:
            logger.info(full_cmd)

            is_external_tool = paths is not None and not any(
                cmd_path.startswith(str(path)) for path in paths
            )
            if is_external_tool:
                if external == "error":
                    logger.error(
                        f"Error: {cmd} is not installed into the virtualenv, it is located"
                        f" at {cmd_path}. Pass external=True into run() to explicitly allow"
                        " this."
                    )
                    msg = "External program disallowed."
                    raise CommandFailed(msg)
                if external is False:
                    logger.warning(
                        f"Warning: {cmd} is not installed into the virtualenv, it is"
                        f" located at {cmd_path}. This might cause issues! Pass"
                        " external=True into run() to silence this message."
                    )

        env = _clean_env(env)

        try:
            return_code, output = popen(
                [cmd_path, *str_args],
                silent=silent,
                env=env,
                stdout=stdout,
                stderr=stderr,
                interrupt_timeout=interrupt_timeout,
                terminate_timeout=terminate_timeout,
            )

            if return_code not in success_codes:
                suffix = ":" if (silent and output) else ""
                logger.error(
                    f"Command {full_cmd} failed with exit code {return_code}{suffix}"
                )

                if silent and output:
                    logger.error(output)

                msg = f"Returned code {return_code}"
>               raise CommandFailed(msg)
E               nox.command.CommandFailed: Returned code 1

        """Call the hook.

        Only accepts keyword arguments, which should match the hook

        Returns the result(s) of calling all registered plugins, see

hook_name = 'pytest_runtest_call'
hook_impls = [<HookImpl plugin_name='runner', plugin=<module '_pytest.runner' from '/app/.nox/minimums-3-11/lib/python3.11/site-pac...ule '_pytest.threadexception' from '/app/.nox/minimums-3-11/lib/python3.11/site-packages/_pytest/threadexception.py'>>]
caller_kwargs = {'item': <Function test_stale_environment[venv-virtualenv-True]>}
firstresult = False

    def _multicall(
        hook_name: str,
        hook_impls: Sequence[HookImpl],
        caller_kwargs: Mapping[str, object],
        firstresult: bool,
    ) -> object | list[object]:
        """Execute a call into multiple python functions/methods and return the
        result(s).

        ``caller_kwargs`` comes from HookCaller.__call__().
        """
        __tracebackhide__ = True
        results: list[object] = []
        exception = None
        try:  # run impl and wrapper setup functions in a loop
            teardowns: list[Teardown] = []
            try:
                for hook_impl in reversed(hook_impls):
                    try:
                        args = [caller_kwargs[argname] for argname in hook_impl.argnames]
                    except KeyError as e:
                        # coverage bug - this is tested
                        for argname in hook_impl.argnames:  # pragma: no cover
                            if argname not in caller_kwargs:
                                raise HookCallError(
                                    f"hook call must provide argument {argname!r}"
                                ) from e

                    if hook_impl.hookwrapper:
                        function_gen = run_old_style_hookwrapper(hook_impl, hook_name, args)

                        next(function_gen)  # first yield
                        teardowns.append(function_gen)

                    elif hook_impl.wrapper:
                        try:
                            # If this cast is not valid, a type error is raised below,
                            # which is the desired response.
                            res = hook_impl.function(*args)
                            function_gen = cast(Generator[None, object, object], res)
                            next(function_gen)  # first yield
                            teardowns.append(function_gen)
                        except StopIteration:
                            _raise_wrapfail(function_gen, "did not yield")
                    else:
                        res = hook_impl.function(*args)
                        if res is not None:
                            results.append(res)
                            if firstresult:  # halt further impl calls
                                break
            except BaseException as exc:
                exception = exc
        finally:
            if firstresult:  # first result hooks return a single value
                result = results[0] if results else None
            else:
                result = results

            # run all wrapper post-yield blocks
            for teardown in reversed(teardowns):
                try:
                    if exception is not None:
                        try:
                            teardown.throw(exception)
                        except RuntimeError as re:
                            # StopIteration from generator causes RuntimeError
                            # even for coroutine usage - see #544
                            if (
                                isinstance(exception, StopIteration)
                                and re.__cause__ is exception
                            ):
                                teardown.close()
                                continue
                            else:
                                raise
                    else:
                        teardown.send(result)
                    # Following is unreachable for a well behaved hook wrapper.
                    # Try to force finalizers otherwise postponed till GC action.
                    # Note: close() may raise if generator handles GeneratorExit.
                    teardown.close()
                except StopIteration as si:
                    result = si.value
                    exception = None
                    continue
                except BaseException as e:
                    exception = e
                    continue
                _raise_wrapfail(teardown, "has second yield")

        if exception is not None:
>           raise exception

hook_impl = <HookImpl plugin_name='threadexception', plugin=<module '_pytest.threadexception' from '/app/.nox/minimums-3-11/lib/python3.11/site-packages/_pytest/threadexception.py'>>
hook_name = 'pytest_runtest_call', args = []

    def run_old_style_hookwrapper(
        hook_impl: HookImpl, hook_name: str, args: Sequence[object]
    ) -> Teardown:
        """
        backward compatibility wrapper to run a old style hookwrapper as a wrapper
        """

        teardown: Teardown = cast(Teardown, hook_impl.function(*args))
        try:
            next(teardown)
        except StopIteration:
            _raise_wrapfail(teardown, "did not yield")
        try:
            res = yield
            result = Result(res, None)
        except BaseException as exc:
            result = Result(None, exc)
        try:
            teardown.send(result)
        except StopIteration:
            pass
        except BaseException as e:
            _warn_teardown_exception(hook_name, hook_impl, e)
            raise
        else:
            _raise_wrapfail(teardown, "has second yield")
        finally:
            teardown.close()
>       return result.get_result()

    def get_result(self) -> ResultType:
        """Get the result(s) for this hook call.

        If the hook was marked as a ``firstresult`` only a single value
        will be returned, otherwise a list of results.
        """
        __tracebackhide__ = True
        exc = self._exception
        tb = self._traceback
        if exc is None:
            return cast(ResultType, self._result)
        else:
>           raise exc.with_traceback(tb)

hook_impls = [<HookImpl plugin_name='runner', plugin=<module '_pytest.runner' from '/app/.nox/minimums-3-11/lib/python3.11/site-pac...ule '_pytest.threadexception' from '/app/.nox/minimums-3-11/lib/python3.11/site-packages/_pytest/threadexception.py'>>]
caller_kwargs = {'item': <Function test_stale_environment[venv-virtualenv-True]>}
firstresult = False

    def _multicall(
        hook_name: str,
        hook_impls: Sequence[HookImpl],
        caller_kwargs: Mapping[str, object],
        firstresult: bool,
    ) -> object | list[object]:
        """Execute a call into multiple python functions/methods and return the
        result(s).

        ``caller_kwargs`` comes from HookCaller.__call__().
        """
        __tracebackhide__ = True
        results: list[object] = []
        exception = None
        try:  # run impl and wrapper setup functions in a loop
            teardowns: list[Teardown] = []
            try:
                for hook_impl in reversed(hook_impls):
                    try:
                        args = [caller_kwargs[argname] for argname in hook_impl.argnames]
                    except KeyError as e:
                        # coverage bug - this is tested
                        for argname in hook_impl.argnames:  # pragma: no cover
                            if argname not in caller_kwargs:
                                raise HookCallError(
                                    f"hook call must provide argument {argname!r}"
                                ) from e

                    if hook_impl.hookwrapper:
                        function_gen = run_old_style_hookwrapper(hook_impl, hook_name, args)

                        next(function_gen)  # first yield
                        teardowns.append(function_gen)

                    elif hook_impl.wrapper:
                        try:
                            # If this cast is not valid, a type error is raised below,
                            # which is the desired response.
                            res = hook_impl.function(*args)
                            function_gen = cast(Generator[None, object, object], res)
                            next(function_gen)  # first yield
                            teardowns.append(function_gen)
                        except StopIteration:
                            _raise_wrapfail(function_gen, "did not yield")
                    else:
                        res = hook_impl.function(*args)
                        if res is not None:
                            results.append(res)
                            if firstresult:  # halt further impl calls
                                break
            except BaseException as exc:
                exception = exc
        finally:
            if firstresult:  # first result hooks return a single value
                result = results[0] if results else None
            else:
                result = results

            # run all wrapper post-yield blocks
            for teardown in reversed(teardowns):
                try:
                    if exception is not None:
                        try:
>                           teardown.throw(exception)

/app/.nox/minimums-3-11/lib/python3.11/site-packages/pluggy/_callers.py:139:

hook_impl = <HookImpl plugin_name='logging-plugin', plugin=<_pytest.logging.LoggingPlugin object at 0x7f0710594050>>
hook_name = 'pytest_runtest_call'
args = [<Function test_stale_environment[venv-virtualenv-True]>]

    def run_old_style_hookwrapper(
        hook_impl: HookImpl, hook_name: str, args: Sequence[object]
    ) -> Teardown:
        """
        backward compatibility wrapper to run a old style hookwrapper as a wrapper
        """

        teardown: Teardown = cast(Teardown, hook_impl.function(*args))
        try:
            next(teardown)
        except StopIteration:
            _raise_wrapfail(teardown, "did not yield")
        try:
            res = yield
            result = Result(res, None)
        except BaseException as exc:
            result = Result(None, exc)
        try:
            teardown.send(result)
        except StopIteration:
            pass
        except BaseException as e:
            _warn_teardown_exception(hook_name, hook_impl, e)
            raise
        else:
            _raise_wrapfail(teardown, "has second yield")
        finally:
            teardown.close()
>       return result.get_result()

        """

        tb = self._traceback
        if exc is None:

        else:

item = <Function test_stale_environment[venv-virtualenv-True]>

    def pytest_runtest_call(item: Item) -> None:
        _update_current_test_var(item, "call")
        try:
            del sys.last_type
            del sys.last_value
            del sys.last_traceback
        except AttributeError:
            pass
        try:
            item.runtest()
        except Exception as e:
            # Store trace info to allow postmortem debugging
            sys.last_type = type(e)
            sys.last_value = e
            assert e.__traceback__ is not None
            # Skip *this* frame
            sys.last_traceback = e.__traceback__.tb_next
>           raise e

self = <HookCaller 'pytest_pyfunc_call'>

firstresult = True

    def __call__(self, **kwargs: object) -> Any:
        """Call the hook.

        Only accepts keyword arguments, which should match the hook
        specification.

        Returns the result(s) of calling all registered plugins, see
        :ref:`calling`.
        """
        assert not self.is_historic(), (
            "Cannot directly call a historic hook - use call_historic instead."
        )
        self._verify_all_args_are_provided(kwargs)
        firstresult = self.spec.opts.get("firstresult", False) if self.spec else False
        # Copy because plugins may register other plugins during iteration (#438).
>       return self._hookexec(self.name, self._hookimpls.copy(), kwargs, firstresult)

                        args = [caller_kwargs[argname] for argname in hook_impl.argnames]
                    except KeyError as e:
                        # coverage bug - this is tested
                        for argname in hook_impl.argnames:  # pragma: no cover
                            if argname not in caller_kwargs:
                                raise HookCallError(
                                    f"hook call must provide argument {argname!r}"
                                ) from e

                    if hook_impl.hookwrapper:
                        function_gen = run_old_style_hookwrapper(hook_impl, hook_name, args)

                        next(function_gen)  # first yield
                        teardowns.append(function_gen)

                    elif hook_impl.wrapper:
                        try:
                            # If this cast is not valid, a type error is raised below,
                            # which is the desired response.
                            res = hook_impl.function(*args)
                            function_gen = cast(Generator[None, object, object], res)
                            next(function_gen)  # first yield
                            teardowns.append(function_gen)
                        except StopIteration:
                            _raise_wrapfail(function_gen, "did not yield")
                    else:
                        res = hook_impl.function(*args)
                        if res is not None:
                            results.append(res)
                            if firstresult:  # halt further impl calls
                                break
            except BaseException as exc:
                exception = exc
        finally:
            if firstresult:  # first result hooks return a single value
                result = results[0] if results else None
            else:
                result = results

            # run all wrapper post-yield blocks
            for teardown in reversed(teardowns):
                try:
                    if exception is not None:
                        try:
                            teardown.throw(exception)
                        except RuntimeError as re:
                            # StopIteration from generator causes RuntimeError
                            # even for coroutine usage - see #544
                            if (
                                isinstance(exception, StopIteration)
                                and re.__cause__ is exception
                            ):
                                teardown.close()
                                continue
                            else:
                                raise
                    else:
                        teardown.send(result)
                    # Following is unreachable for a well behaved hook wrapper.
                    # Try to force finalizers otherwise postponed till GC action.
                    # Note: close() may raise if generator handles GeneratorExit.
                    teardown.close()
                except StopIteration as si:
                    result = si.value
                    exception = None
                    continue
                except BaseException as e:
                    exception = e
                    continue
                _raise_wrapfail(teardown, "has second yield")

        if exception is not None:
>           raise exception

self = <nox.virtualenv.VirtualEnv object at 0x7f070fdf1b10>

    def create(self) -> bool:
        """Create the virtualenv or venv."""
        if not self._clean_location():
            logger.debug(
                f"Reusing existing virtual environment at {self.location_name}."
            )

            self._reused = True

            return False

        if self.venv_backend == "virtualenv":
            cmd = [
                sys.executable,
                "-m",
                "virtualenv",
                self.location,
                "--no-periodic-update",
            ]
            if self.interpreter:
                cmd.extend(["-p", self._resolved_interpreter])
        elif self.venv_backend == "uv":
            cmd = [
                UV,
                "venv",
                "-p",
                self._resolved_interpreter if self.interpreter else sys.executable,
                self.location,
            ]
            if version.Version("0.8") <= UV_VERSION:
                cmd += ["--clear"]
        else:
            cmd = [self._resolved_interpreter, "-m", "venv", self.location]
        cmd.extend(self.venv_params)

        resolved_interpreter_name = os.path.basename(self._resolved_interpreter)

        logger.info(
            f"Creating virtual environment ({self.venv_backend}) using"
            f" {resolved_interpreter_name} in {self.location_name}"
        )
>       nox.command.run(cmd, silent=True, log=nox.options.verbose or False)

    def run(
        args: Sequence[str | os.PathLike[str]],
        *,
        env: Mapping[str, str | None] | None = None,
        silent: bool = False,
        paths: Sequence[str | os.PathLike[str]] | None = None,
        success_codes: Iterable[int] | None = None,
        log: bool = True,
        external: ExternalType = False,
        stdout: int | IO[str] | None = None,
        stderr: int | IO[str] | None = subprocess.STDOUT,
        interrupt_timeout: float | None = DEFAULT_INTERRUPT_TIMEOUT,
        terminate_timeout: float | None = DEFAULT_TERMINATE_TIMEOUT,
    ) -> str | bool:
        """Run a command-line program."""

        if success_codes is None:
            success_codes = [0]

        cmd, args = args[0], args[1:]
        full_cmd = f"{cmd} {_shlex_join(args)}"

        cmd_path = which(os.fspath(cmd), paths)
        str_args = [os.fspath(arg) for arg in args]

        if log:
            logger.info(full_cmd)

            is_external_tool = paths is not None and not any(
                cmd_path.startswith(str(path)) for path in paths
            )
            if is_external_tool:
                if external == "error":
                    logger.error(
                        f"Error: {cmd} is not installed into the virtualenv, it is located"
                        f" at {cmd_path}. Pass external=True into run() to explicitly allow"
                        " this."
                    )
                    msg = "External program disallowed."
                    raise CommandFailed(msg)
                if external is False:
                    logger.warning(
                        f"Warning: {cmd} is not installed into the virtualenv, it is"
                        f" located at {cmd_path}. This might cause issues! Pass"
                        " external=True into run() to silence this message."
                    )

        env = _clean_env(env)

        try:
            return_code, output = popen(
                [cmd_path, *str_args],
                silent=silent,
                env=env,
                stdout=stdout,
                stderr=stderr,
                interrupt_timeout=interrupt_timeout,
                terminate_timeout=terminate_timeout,
            )

            if return_code not in success_codes:
                suffix = ":" if (silent and output) else ""
                logger.error(
                    f"Command {full_cmd} failed with exit code {return_code}{suffix}"
                )

                if silent and output:
                    logger.error(output)

                msg = f"Returned code {return_code}"
>               raise CommandFailed(msg)

    def __call__(self, **kwargs: object) -> Any:
        """Call the hook.

        Only accepts keyword arguments, which should match the hook
        specification.

hook_impl = <HookImpl plugin_name='threadexception', plugin=<module '_pytest.threadexception' from '/app/.nox/minimums-3-11/lib/python3.11/site-packages/_pytest/threadexception.py'>>
hook_name = 'pytest_runtest_call', args = []

    def run_old_style_hookwrapper(
        hook_impl: HookImpl, hook_name: str, args: Sequence[object]
    ) -> Teardown:
        """
        backward compatibility wrapper to run a old style hookwrapper as a wrapper
        """

        teardown: Teardown = cast(Teardown, hook_impl.function(*args))
        try:
            next(teardown)
        except StopIteration:
            _raise_wrapfail(teardown, "did not yield")
        try:
            res = yield
            result = Result(res, None)
        except BaseException as exc:
            result = Result(None, exc)
        try:
            teardown.send(result)
        except StopIteration:
            pass
        except BaseException as e:
            _warn_teardown_exception(hook_name, hook_impl, e)
            raise
        else:
            _raise_wrapfail(teardown, "has second yield")
        finally:
            teardown.close()
>       return result.get_result()

    def get_result(self) -> ResultType:
        """Get the result(s) for this hook call.

        If the hook was marked as a ``firstresult`` only a single value
        will be returned, otherwise a list of results.
        """

        exc = self._exception
        tb = self._traceback
        if exc is None:

        else:

/app/.nox/minimums-3-11/lib/python3.11/site-packages/pluggy/_callers.py:38:
_ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _

hook_name = 'pytest_runtest_call'
hook_impls = [<HookImpl plugin_name='runner', plugin=<module '_pytest.runner' from '/app/.nox/minimums-3-11/lib/python3.11/site-pac...ule '_pytest.threadexception' from '/app/.nox/minimums-3-11/lib/python3.11/site-packages/_pytest/threadexception.py'>>]
caller_kwargs = {'item': <Function test_create_reuse_stale_virtualenv_environment>}
firstresult = False

    def _multicall(
        hook_name: str,
        hook_impls: Sequence[HookImpl],
        caller_kwargs: Mapping[str, object],
        firstresult: bool,
    ) -> object | list[object]:
        """Execute a call into multiple python functions/methods and return the
        result(s).

        ``caller_kwargs`` comes from HookCaller.__call__().
        """
        __tracebackhide__ = True
        results: list[object] = []
        exception = None
        try:  # run impl and wrapper setup functions in a loop
            teardowns: list[Teardown] = []
            try:
                for hook_impl in reversed(hook_impls):
                    try:
                        args = [caller_kwargs[argname] for argname in hook_impl.argnames]
                    except KeyError as e:
                        # coverage bug - this is tested
                        for argname in hook_impl.argnames:  # pragma: no cover
                            if argname not in caller_kwargs:
                                raise HookCallError(
                                    f"hook call must provide argument {argname!r}"
                                ) from e

                    if hook_impl.hookwrapper:
                        function_gen = run_old_style_hookwrapper(hook_impl, hook_name, args)

                        next(function_gen)  # first yield
                        teardowns.append(function_gen)

                    elif hook_impl.wrapper:
                        try:
                            # If this cast is not valid, a type error is raised below,
                            # which is the desired response.
                            res = hook_impl.function(*args)
                            function_gen = cast(Generator[None, object, object], res)
                            next(function_gen)  # first yield
                            teardowns.append(function_gen)
                        except StopIteration:
                            _raise_wrapfail(function_gen, "did not yield")
                    else:
                        res = hook_impl.function(*args)
                        if res is not None:
                            results.append(res)
                            if firstresult:  # halt further impl calls
                                break
            except BaseException as exc:
                exception = exc
        finally:
            if firstresult:  # first result hooks return a single value
                result = results[0] if results else None
            else:
                result = results

            # run all wrapper post-yield blocks
            for teardown in reversed(teardowns):
                try:
                    if exception is not None:
                        try:
>                           teardown.throw(exception)

/app/.nox/minimums-3-11/lib/python3.11/site-packages/pluggy/_callers.py:139:
_ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _

hook_impl = <HookImpl plugin_name='unraisableexception', plugin=<module '_pytest.unraisableexception' from '/app/.nox/minimums-3-11/lib/python3.11/site-packages/_pytest/unraisableexception.py'>>
hook_name = 'pytest_runtest_call', args = []

    def run_old_style_hookwrapper(
        hook_impl: HookImpl, hook_name: str, args: Sequence[object]
    ) -> Teardown:
        """
        backward compatibility wrapper to run a old style hookwrapper as a wrapper
        """

        teardown: Teardown = cast(Teardown, hook_impl.function(*args))
        try:
            next(teardown)
        except StopIteration:
            _raise_wrapfail(teardown, "did not yield")
        try:
            res = yield
            result = Result(res, None)
        except BaseException as exc:
            result = Result(None, exc)
        try:
            teardown.send(result)
        except StopIteration:
            pass
        except BaseException as e:
            _warn_teardown_exception(hook_name, hook_impl, e)
            raise
        else:
            _raise_wrapfail(teardown, "has second yield")
        finally:
            teardown.close()
>       return result.get_result()

self = <pluggy._result.Result object at 0x7f070feabd80>

    def get_result(self) -> ResultType:
        """Get the result(s) for this hook call.

        If the hook was marked as a ``firstresult`` only a single value
        will be returned, otherwise a list of results.
        """
        __tracebackhide__ = True
        exc = self._exception
        tb = self._traceback
        if exc is None:
            return cast(ResultType, self._result)
        else:
>           raise exc.with_traceback(tb)

    def pytest_runtest_call(item: Item) -> None:
        _update_current_test_var(item, "call")
        try:
            del sys.last_type
            del sys.last_value
            del sys.last_traceback
        except AttributeError:
            pass
        try:
            item.runtest()
        except Exception as e:
            # Store trace info to allow postmortem debugging
            sys.last_type = type(e)
            sys.last_value = e
            assert e.__traceback__ is not None
            # Skip *this* frame
            sys.last_traceback = e.__traceback__.tb_next
>           raise e

hook_name = 'pytest_pyfunc_call'
hook_impls = [<HookImpl plugin_name='python', plugin=<module '_pytest.python' from '/app/.nox/minimums-3-11/lib/python3.11/site-packages/_pytest/python.py'>>]
caller_kwargs = {'pyfuncitem': <Function test_create_reuse_stale_virtualenv_environment>}
firstresult = True

    def _multicall(
        hook_name: str,
        hook_impls: Sequence[HookImpl],
        caller_kwargs: Mapping[str, object],
        firstresult: bool,
    ) -> object | list[object]:
        """Execute a call into multiple python functions/methods and return the
        result(s).

        ``caller_kwargs`` comes from HookCaller.__call__().
        """
        __tracebackhide__ = True
        results: list[object] = []
        exception = None
        try:  # run impl and wrapper setup functions in a loop
            teardowns: list[Teardown] = []
            try:
                for hook_impl in reversed(hook_impls):
                    try:
                        args = [caller_kwargs[argname] for argname in hook_impl.argnames]
                    except KeyError as e:
                        # coverage bug - this is tested
                        for argname in hook_impl.argnames:  # pragma: no cover
                            if argname not in caller_kwargs:
                                raise HookCallError(
                                    f"hook call must provide argument {argname!r}"
                                ) from e

                    if hook_impl.hookwrapper:
                        function_gen = run_old_style_hookwrapper(hook_impl, hook_name, args)

                        next(function_gen)  # first yield
                        teardowns.append(function_gen)

                    elif hook_impl.wrapper:
                        try:
                            # If this cast is not valid, a type error is raised below,
                            # which is the desired response.
                            res = hook_impl.function(*args)
                            function_gen = cast(Generator[None, object, object], res)
                            next(function_gen)  # first yield
                            teardowns.append(function_gen)
                        except StopIteration:
                            _raise_wrapfail(function_gen, "did not yield")
                    else:
                        res = hook_impl.function(*args)
                        if res is not None:
                            results.append(res)
                            if firstresult:  # halt further impl calls
                                break
            except BaseException as exc:
                exception = exc
        finally:
            if firstresult:  # first result hooks return a single value
                result = results[0] if results else None
            else:
                result = results

            # run all wrapper post-yield blocks
            for teardown in reversed(teardowns):
                try:
                    if exception is not None:
                        try:
                            teardown.throw(exception)
                        except RuntimeError as re:
                            # StopIteration from generator causes RuntimeError
                            # even for coroutine usage - see #544
                            if (
                                isinstance(exception, StopIteration)
                                and re.__cause__ is exception
                            ):
                                teardown.close()
                                continue
                            else:
                                raise
                    else:
                        teardown.send(result)
                    # Following is unreachable for a well behaved hook wrapper.
                    # Try to force finalizers otherwise postponed till GC action.
                    # Note: close() may raise if generator handles GeneratorExit.
                    teardown.close()
                except StopIteration as si:
                    result = si.value
                    exception = None
                    continue
                except BaseException as e:
                    exception = e
                    continue
                _raise_wrapfail(teardown, "has second yield")

        if exception is not None:
>           raise exception

/app/tests/test_virtualenv.py:705:

self = <nox.virtualenv.VirtualEnv object at 0x7f070f8f4c50>

    def create(self) -> bool:
        """Create the virtualenv or venv."""
        if not self._clean_location():
            logger.debug(
                f"Reusing existing virtual environment at {self.location_name}."
            )

            self._reused = True

            return False

        if self.venv_backend == "virtualenv":
            cmd = [
                sys.executable,
                "-m",
                "virtualenv",
                self.location,
                "--no-periodic-update",
            ]
            if self.interpreter:
                cmd.extend(["-p", self._resolved_interpreter])
        elif self.venv_backend == "uv":
            cmd = [
                UV,
                "venv",
                "-p",
                self._resolved_interpreter if self.interpreter else sys.executable,
                self.location,
            ]
            if version.Version("0.8") <= UV_VERSION:
                cmd += ["--clear"]
        else:
            cmd = [self._resolved_interpreter, "-m", "venv", self.location]
        cmd.extend(self.venv_params)

        resolved_interpreter_name = os.path.basename(self._resolved_interpreter)

        logger.info(
            f"Creating virtual environment ({self.venv_backend}) using"
            f" {resolved_interpreter_name} in {self.location_name}"
        )
>       nox.command.run(cmd, silent=True, log=nox.options.verbose or False)

/app/nox/virtualenv.py:817:

args = ['-m', 'venv', '/app/.nox/minimums-3-11/tmp/pytest-of-root/pytest-0/test_create_reuse_stale_virtua0/venv']

    def run(
        args: Sequence[str | os.PathLike[str]],
        *,
        env: Mapping[str, str | None] | None = None,
        silent: bool = False,
        paths: Sequence[str | os.PathLike[str]] | None = None,
        success_codes: Iterable[int] | None = None,
        log: bool = True,
        external: ExternalType = False,
        stdout: int | IO[str] | None = None,
        stderr: int | IO[str] | None = subprocess.STDOUT,
        interrupt_timeout: float | None = DEFAULT_INTERRUPT_TIMEOUT,
        terminate_timeout: float | None = DEFAULT_TERMINATE_TIMEOUT,
    ) -> str | bool:
        """Run a command-line program."""

        if success_codes is None:
            success_codes = [0]

        cmd, args = args[0], args[1:]
        full_cmd = f"{cmd} {_shlex_join(args)}"

        cmd_path = which(os.fspath(cmd), paths)
        str_args = [os.fspath(arg) for arg in args]

        if log:
            logger.info(full_cmd)

            is_external_tool = paths is not None and not any(
                cmd_path.startswith(str(path)) for path in paths
            )
            if is_external_tool:
                if external == "error":
                    logger.error(
                        f"Error: {cmd} is not installed into the virtualenv, it is located"
                        f" at {cmd_path}. Pass external=True into run() to explicitly allow"
                        " this."
                    )
                    msg = "External program disallowed."
                    raise CommandFailed(msg)
                if external is False:
                    logger.warning(
                        f"Warning: {cmd} is not installed into the virtualenv, it is"
                        f" located at {cmd_path}. This might cause issues! Pass"
                        " external=True into run() to silence this message."
                    )

        env = _clean_env(env)

        try:
            return_code, output = popen(
                [cmd_path, *str_args],
                silent=silent,
                env=env,
                stdout=stdout,
                stderr=stderr,
                interrupt_timeout=interrupt_timeout,
                terminate_timeout=terminate_timeout,
            )

            if return_code not in success_codes:
                suffix = ":" if (silent and output) else ""
                logger.error(
                    f"Command {full_cmd} failed with exit code {return_code}{suffix}"
                )

                if silent and output:
                    logger.error(output)

                msg = f"Returned code {return_code}"
>               raise CommandFailed(msg)
